<div class="wpml-ls-statics-shortcode_actions wpml-ls wpml-ls-legacy-list-horizontal">
	<ul><li class="wpml-ls-slot-shortcode_actions wpml-ls-item wpml-ls-item-en wpml-ls-current-language wpml-ls-first-item wpml-ls-item-legacy-list-horizontal">

<script>
jQuery(document).ready(function () {
	var previousScroll = 0;
	jQuery(window).scroll(function () {
		var currentScroll = jQuery(this).scrollTop();
		if (currentScroll < 100) {
			showNav();
		} else if (currentScroll > 0 && currentScroll < jQuery(document).height() - jQuery(window).height()) {
			if (currentScroll > previousScroll) {
				hideNav();
			} else {
				showNav();
			}
			previousScroll = currentScroll;
		}
	});

	function hideNav() {
		jQuery(".header-menu-mobile").removeClass("is-visible").addClass("is-hidden");
	}

	function showNav() {
		jQuery(".header-menu-mobile").removeClass("is-hidden").addClass("is-visible").addClass("scrolling");
	}
});
</script>



<script>
    jQuery(function(){
    jQuery(window).scroll(function(){
        if(jQuery(this).scrollTop() > 100){
          jQuery('.desktop-header').addClass('fixed-header');
          jQuery('.hide-scroll').addClass('none');
        }
        else{
          jQuery('.desktop-header').removeClass('fixed-header');
          jQuery('.hide-scroll').removeClass('none');
        }
    });
});

</script>

        const map = new google.maps.Map(document.getElementById("desktop-map"), {
            center: { lat: parseFloat(locations[0].latitude), lng: parseFloat(locations[0].longitude) },
            zoom: 12,
            streetViewControl: false,
            mapTypeControl: false
        });

        locations.forEach(location => {
            let contentString = `<div class="location-name font-bold text-base mb-1">${location.title}</div>`;
            contentString += `<div class="location-address-name mb-1">`;
            contentString += `${location.address}<br>`;
            contentString += `${location.city}, ${location.state} ${location.zip}</div>`;
            contentString += `<div class="location-permalink"><a href="${location.permalink}" class="text-blue">View More Details</a></div>`;

            let marker = new google.maps.Marker({
                position: { lat: parseFloat(location.latitude), lng: parseFloat(location.longitude) },
                map: map
            });
            let infowindow = new google.maps.InfoWindow({
                content: contentString,
            });
            marker.addListener("click", () => {
                if( prev_infowindow ) {
                    prev_infowindow.close();
                }
                prev_infowindow = infowindow;
                infowindow.open({
                    anchor: marker,
                    map,
                    shouldFocus: false,
                });
            });
        });
    });
</script>

<script>
    var firstVisit = true;
    if ('scrollRestoration' in history) {
        history.scrollRestoration = 'manual';
    }
    jQuery(window).scroll(function() {
        if (firstVisit) {
            window.scrollTo(0, 0);
            firstVisit = false;
            console.log('scroll top')
        }
    });
    jQuery(window).load(function(){
        if(window.location.hash && jQuery(window).width() < 768) {
            console.log(jQuery(window.location.hash).offset().top)
            jQuery('html, body').animate({
                scrollTop: jQuery(window.location.hash).offset().top + 'px'
            }, 2000, 'swing');
        }
    });
    function formatTypeState (data) {
        let allTypeIcons = [];
                allTypeIcons.push('https://www.harvesters.org/wp-content/uploads/2021/06/key-icon-pantry.png')
                allTypeIcons.push('https://www.harvesters.org/wp-content/uploads/2021/06/key-icon-drive-thru.png')
                allTypeIcons.push('https://www.harvesters.org/wp-content/uploads/2021/06/key-icon-kitchen.png')
                if (!data.id) {
            var $state = '<div class="flex items-center justify-between w-full h-select-container"><div class="pr-2 flex-shrink whitespace-no-wrap">All Types</div><div class="flex flex-grow justify-end items-start">';
            allTypeIcons.forEach(icon => {
                $state += '<img src="' + icon + '" class="select-icon-image mx-1" alt="' + data.text + '" />';
            });
            $state += '</div></div>';

            return jQuery($state);
        }
        const el = data.element;
        const iconUrl = jQuery(el).attr('data-icon-url');
        var $state = jQuery(
            '<div class="flex items-center justify-between h-select-container w-full"><div class="pr-2">' + data.text + '</div> <img src="' + iconUrl + '" class="select-icon-image" /></div>'
        );
        return $state;
    };

    jQuery(document).ready(function() {
      jQuery('#selectradius').select2({
        minimumResultsForSearch: Infinity
      });

      jQuery('#selecttype').select2({
        templateResult: formatTypeState,
        templateSelection: formatTypeState,
        minimumResultsForSearch: Infinity
      });
    });
</script>

		<script type="text/javascript">
			var visualizerUserInteractionEvents = [
				"scroll",
				"mouseover",
				"keydown",
				"touchmove",
				"touchstart"
			];

			visualizerUserInteractionEvents.forEach(function(event) {
				window.addEventListener(event, visualizerTriggerScriptLoader, { passive: true });
			});

			function visualizerTriggerScriptLoader() {
				visualizerLoadScripts();
				visualizerUserInteractionEvents.forEach(function(event) {
					window.removeEventListener(event, visualizerTriggerScriptLoader, { passive: true });
				});
			}

			function visualizerLoadScripts() {
				document.querySelectorAll("script[data-visualizer-script]").forEach(function(elem) {
					jQuery.getScript( elem.getAttribute("data-visualizer-script") )
					.done( function( script, textStatus ) {
						elem.setAttribute("src", elem.getAttribute("data-visualizer-script"));
						elem.removeAttribute("data-visualizer-script");
						setTimeout( function() {
							visualizerRefreshChart();
						} );
					} );
				});
			}

			function visualizerRefreshChart() {
				jQuery( '.visualizer-front:not(.visualizer-chart-loaded)' ).resize();
				if ( jQuery( 'div.viz-facade-loaded:not(.visualizer-lazy):empty' ).length > 0 ) {
					visualizerUserInteractionEvents.forEach( function( event ) {
						window.addEventListener( event, function() {
							jQuery( '.visualizer-front:not(.visualizer-chart-loaded)' ).resize();
						}, { passive: true } );
					} );
				}
			}
		</script>
